<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle {\begin{aligned}y&amp;=x^{2}\\{\frac {\mathrm {d} y}{\mathrm {d} x}}&amp;=2x.\end{aligned}}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="
\begin{align}
y&amp;=x^2 \\
\frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{d}x}&amp;=2x.
\end{align}
" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/50feb8ee88bddcc13767d995f1d438491bd2d42d" style="vertical-align: -3.838ex; width:10.447ex; height:8.843ex;"/></span></dd></dl>
<p>在以<a href="/wiki/%E6%9E%81%E9%99%90_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)" title="极限 (数学)">极限</a>为基础的理论里，记号<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle {\frac {\mathrm {d} y}{\mathrm {d} x}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mfrac>
<mrow>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi mathvariant="normal">d</mi>
</mrow>
<mi>y</mi>
</mrow>
<mrow>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi mathvariant="normal">d</mi>
</mrow>
<mi>x</mi>
</mrow>
</mfrac>
</mrow>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle {\frac {\mathrm {d} y}{\mathrm {d} x}}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\frac{\mathrm{d}y}{\mathrm{d}x}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/5bbde3ef39cc332ea2d64427d1a79476bd2b7484" style="vertical-align: -2.005ex; width:3.458ex; height:5.509ex;"/></span>并不理解成两个数的商，而是上面计算的极限的简记。然而，莱布尼茨打算将它表示成两个<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%97%A0%E7%A9%B7%E5%B0%8F" title="无穷小">无穷小</a>數的商，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle x}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>x</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle x}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="x" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/87f9e315fd7e2ba406057a97300593c4802b53e4" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.33ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>的一个无穷小变化量<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \mathrm {d} x}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi mathvariant="normal">d</mi>
</mrow>
<mi>x</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \mathrm {d} x}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\mathrm{d}x" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/0b637d7a6d64d797391d40ceae9e8696e5d76f15" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:2.622ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>引起了一个无穷小的变化量<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \mathrm {d} y}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi mathvariant="normal">d</mi>
</mrow>
<mi>y</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \mathrm {d} y}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\mathrm{d}y" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/40ec4b0f294f77937ccbd41e91214ba60b67ac65" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:2.448ex; height:2.509ex;"/></span>。我们也可以把<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle {\frac {\mathrm {d} }{\mathrm {d} x}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mfrac>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi mathvariant="normal">d</mi>
</mrow>
<mrow>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi mathvariant="normal">d</mi>
</mrow>
<mi>x</mi>
</mrow>
</mfrac>
</mrow>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle {\frac {\mathrm {d} }{\mathrm {d} x}}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\frac{\mathrm{d}}{\mathrm{d}x}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/0653947153193a81f93e4e8e286c737e220c7ac5" style="vertical-align: -2.005ex; width:3.458ex; height:5.509ex;"/></span>看作一个微分算子，它以一个函数为输入，以这个函数的导函数作为输出。例如：
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle {\frac {\mathrm {d} }{\mathrm {d} x}}(x^{2})=2x.}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mfrac>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi mathvariant="normal">d</mi>
</mrow>
<mrow>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi mathvariant="normal">d</mi>
</mrow>
<mi>x</mi>
</mrow>
</mfrac>
</mrow>
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<msup>
<mi>x</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>2</mn>
</mrow>
</msup>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
<mo>=</mo>
<mn>2</mn>
<mi>x</mi>
<mo>.</mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle {\frac {\mathrm {d} }{\mathrm {d} x}}(x^{2})=2x.}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="
\frac{\mathrm{d}}{\mathrm{d}x}(x^2)=2x.
" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9d2a4c2f5eb68207f2c64fdcaa37ffca10f1c3b7" style="vertical-align: -2.005ex; width:13.889ex; height:5.509ex;"/></span></dd></dl>
<p>在这个用法中，分母中的<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \mathrm {d} x}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi mathvariant="normal">d</mi>
</mrow>
<mi>x</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \mathrm {d} x}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\mathrm{d}x" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/0b637d7a6d64d797391d40ceae9e8696e5d76f15" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:2.622ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>读作“关于x”。即使<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%BE%AE%E7%A7%AF%E5%88%86" title="微积分">微积分</a>理论是用<a href="/wiki/%E6%9E%81%E9%99%90_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)" title="极限 (数学)">极限</a>的概念，而不是用<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%97%A0%E7%A9%B7%E5%B0%8F" title="无穷小">无穷小</a>的概念发展成的，人们還是常常把<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \mathrm {d} x}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi mathvariant="normal">d</mi>
</mrow>
<mi>x</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \mathrm {d} x}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\mathrm{d}x" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/0b637d7a6d64d797391d40ceae9e8696e5d76f15" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:2.622ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \mathrm {d} y}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi mathvariant="normal">d</mi>
</mrow>
<mi>y</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \mathrm {d} y}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\mathrm{d}y" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/40ec4b0f294f77937ccbd41e91214ba60b67ac65" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:2.448ex; height:2.509ex;"/></span>这类记号当作實數来操作。尽管可以避免这样的操作，但是有时候它们在符号上可以方便地表达<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%85%A8%E5%AF%BC%E6%95%B0" title="全导数">全导数</a>这类操作。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E7.A9.8D.E5.88.86.E5.AD.B8"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="積分學">積分學</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%BE%AE%E7%A7%AF%E5%88%86%E5%AD%A6&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="编辑章节：積分學">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">主条目：<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%A7%AF%E5%88%86%E5%AD%A6" title="积分学">積分學</a></div>
<p>積分是微分的逆運算，即從導數推算出原函數，又分為定積分與不定積分。一個一元函數的定積分可以定義為無窮多小矩形的面積和，即等於<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B8" title="函數">函數</a>曲線下包含的實際面積。我們也可以用積分來計算平面上一條曲線所包含的面積、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%90%83%E9%AB%94" title="球體">球體</a>或<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%9C%86%E9%94%A5%E4%BD%93" title="圆锥体">圓錐體</a>的表面積或體積等。从技术上来讲，积分学是研究對這兩個相關的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%BA%BF%E6%80%A7%E7%AE%97%E5%AD%90" title="线性算子">线性算子</a>的研究。
</p><p>不定积分是导数的逆运算，即<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%8F%8D%E5%B0%8E%E6%95%B8" title="反導數">反导数</a>。当<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle f}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>f</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle f}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="f" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/132e57acb643253e7810ee9702d9581f159a1c61" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:1.279ex; height:2.509ex;"/></span>是<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle F}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>F</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle F}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="F" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/545fd099af8541605f7ee55f08225526be88ce57" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.741ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>的导数时，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle F}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>F</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle F}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="F" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/545fd099af8541605f7ee55f08225526be88ce57" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.741ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>是<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle f}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>f</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle f}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="f" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/132e57acb643253e7810ee9702d9581f159a1c61" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:1.279ex; height:2.509ex;"/></span>的不定积分。（这种在公式中使用大小写字母以区分微分积分在数学中很常见。）
</p><p>定积分输入公式，输出数字，即给出图像与<a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%A8%AA%E5%9D%90%E6%A0%87&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="横坐标（页面不存在）">横坐标</a>之间各個面积的代数和。对定积分的技术定义是各個矩形之面积和的<a href="/wiki/%E6%9E%81%E9%99%90_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)" title="极限 (数学)">极限</a>，又称<a href="/wiki/%E9%BB%8E%E6%9B%BC%E7%A7%AF%E5%88%86" title="黎曼积分">黎曼积分</a>。
</p><p>举例：在给定时间内行径的路程：
</p><p><b><big>路程 = 速度 × 时间</big></b>
</p><p>如果速度是一定的，那么上述参数简单相乘即可得出结果。但如果速度为变量，那么就不得不使用更强大的公式。其中的一个方式是将行径路程根据时间近似地划分成许多小部分，将每个间距中的时间乘以当时的速度，最后将每个间距所行径的近似路程累计为<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%BB%8E%E6%9B%BC%E5%92%8C" title="黎曼和">黎曼和</a>。當中的基本想法是，如果时长间隔很短，那么速度会近似不变。然而，黎曼和只给出行径路程的近似值。我们必须對所有可能的黎曼和取極限，来得出精确的值。
</p>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:282px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Integral_as_region_under_curve.svg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="700" data-file-width="750" decoding="async" height="261" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f2/Integral_as_region_under_curve.svg/280px-Integral_as_region_under_curve.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f2/Integral_as_region_under_curve.svg/420px-Integral_as_region_under_curve.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f2/Integral_as_region_under_curve.svg/560px-Integral_as_region_under_curve.svg.png 2x" width="280"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Integral_as_region_under_curve.svg" title="放大"></a></div>积分可以被视为在两点之间（这里是<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

</semantics>

<p>如果左图中的<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle f(x)}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<semantics>

</math></span><img alt="b" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/f11423fbb2e967f986e36804a8ae4271734917c3" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:0.998ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>时间点之间的路程就可以用阴影区域<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle s}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</p><p>要求得区域面积的近似值，直观的办法就是将<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>

<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle f(x)=h}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="f(x)=h" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/cc077617937298d33d7e0184b60e1098a6d61d96" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:8.855ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span>。所有矩形的总和就是数轴与曲线之间面积的近似值，即总行径路程的近似值。<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \Delta x}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi mathvariant="normal">Δ<!-- Δ --></mi>
<mi>x</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \Delta x}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\Delta x" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/f3890eb866b6258d7a304fc34c70ee3fb3a81a70" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:3.266ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>的值越小，矩形数量就越多，近似值也就越精确。而如果我们要求得精确值，就必须寻找<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \Delta x}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi mathvariant="normal">Δ<!-- Δ --></mi>
<mi>x</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \Delta x}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\Delta x" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/f3890eb866b6258d7a304fc34c70ee3fb3a81a70" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:3.266ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>的极限，令其数值逼近零。
</p><p>积分的符号是<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \int \,}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mo>∫<!-- ∫ --></mo>
<mspace width="thinmathspace"></mspace>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \int \,}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\int \," aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/ba2794e142343d3783e2163fcebe1f6bcb028f9e" style="vertical-align: -2.338ex; width:2.581ex; height:5.676ex;"/></span>，像一个拉长的<i>S</i>（<i>S</i>意味「求和」，sum）。定积分被记为如下：
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \int _{a}^{b}f(x)\,\mathrm {d} x.}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<mi>b</mi>
</mrow>
</msubsup>
<mi>f</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mi>x</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
<mspace width="thinmathspace"></mspace>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi mathvariant="normal">d</mi>
</mrow>
<mi>x</mi>
<mo>.</mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \int _{a}^{b}f(x)\,\mathrm {d} x.}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\int_a^b f(x)\, \mathrm{d}x." aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/71593af21b1d4adf3e81fee0269933047e936369" style="vertical-align: -2.338ex; width:11.863ex; height:6.343ex;"/></span></dd></dl>
<p>讀作，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle f(x)}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<mi>x</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle f(x)}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="f(x)" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/202945cce41ecebb6f643f31d119c514bec7a074" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:4.418ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span>由<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>

</mstyle>
</mrow>

</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="a" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/ffd2487510aa438433a2579450ab2b3d557e5edc" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.23ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>到<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle b}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">

</mstyle>
</mrow>

</semantics>

<semantics>

</mrow>
<mi>x</mi>
</mstyle>

<mi>x</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \Delta x}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\Delta x" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/f3890eb866b6258d7a304fc34c70ee3fb3a81a70" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:3.266ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>变成无穷小的<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \mathrm {d} x}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \int _{a}^{b}\ldots \,\mathrm {d} x}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>a</mi>
</mrow>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi>b</mi>
</mrow>
</msubsup>
<mo>…<!-- … --></mo>
<mspace width="thinmathspace"></mspace>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

</mrow>
<mi>x</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \int _{a}^{b}\ldots \,\mathrm {d} x}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\int_a^b \ldots\, \mathrm{d}x" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/6f8dc973b6ea6ba857f6b41114eec64e819f2141" style="vertical-align: -2.338ex; width:9.909ex; height:6.343ex;"/></span></dd></dl>
<p>应被理解为一個输入函數，输出数字（即面積）的算子。在终端的微分<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \mathrm {d} x}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi mathvariant="normal">d</mi>
</mrow>
<mi>x</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \mathrm {d} x}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\mathrm{d}x" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/0b637d7a6d64d797391d40ceae9e8696e5d76f15" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:2.622ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>不是数字，也不是与<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle f(x)}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>f</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mi>x</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle f(x)}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="f(x)" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/202945cce41ecebb6f643f31d119c514bec7a074" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:4.418ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span>相乘—雖然，若作为<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \Delta x}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi mathvariant="normal">Δ<!-- Δ --></mi>
<mi>x</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \Delta x}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\Delta x" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/f3890eb866b6258d7a304fc34c70ee3fb3a81a70" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:3.266ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>极限定义的提醒，可理解為积分裡符號运算的相乘。从形式上来讲，微分說明了函數是關於哪個变量被積分。此外，亦作为积分算子的尾括弧。
</p><p>不定积分，或反导数，记作：
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \int f(x)\,\mathrm {d} x.}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">

<mi>f</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mi>x</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
<mspace width="thinmathspace"></mspace>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi mathvariant="normal">d</mi>
</mrow>
<mi>x</mi>
<mo>.</mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \int f(x)\,\mathrm {d} x.}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\int f(x)\, \mathrm{d}x." aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/cbc1fd7129f708f2a4016ee9a672cf265a7780c7" style="vertical-align: -2.338ex; width:10.654ex; height:5.676ex;"/></span></dd></dl>
<p>只相差一個常數的函數有著相同的導數，另外也可以證明一个給定函數的反导数实际上是一個只相差一常数的方程组。例如，考慮函數<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle y=x^{2}+C}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>y</mi>
<mo>=</mo>
<msup>
<mi>x</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>2</mn>
</mrow>
</msup>
<mo>+</mo>
<mi>C</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle y=x^{2}+C}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="y=x^2+C" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/2ae3efd8ac816616f4e3c0958d0f84e0fa6df3b5" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:11.245ex; height:3.009ex;"/></span>，當中<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle C}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

<mi>C</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>

</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="C" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/4fc55753007cd3c18576f7933f6f089196732029" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.766ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>為任意常數，則其導數均為<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle y'=2x}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<msup>

<mo>′</mo>
</msup>
<mo>=</mo>
<mn>2</mn>
<mi>x</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle y'=2x}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="y'=2x" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/e02249b02abfd48ed2ab1a1154ba3c689dcd5869" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:7.436ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span>；后者的反导数可被写为：
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \int 2x\,\mathrm {d} x=x^{2}+C.}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<mspace width="thinmathspace"></mspace>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

</mrow>
<mi>x</mi>
<mo>=</mo>
<msup>

<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>2</mn>
</mrow>
</msup>
<mo>+</mo>
<mi>C</mi>
<mo>.</mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \int 2x\,\mathrm {d} x=x^{2}+C.}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\int 2x\, \mathrm{d}x = x^2 + C." aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/2458681b2adb388a35dbb0227ad05d721796f0b1" style="vertical-align: -2.338ex; width:18.818ex; height:5.676ex;"/></span></dd></dl>
<p>反导数中的未知常数<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle C}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>C</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle C}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="C" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/4fc55753007cd3c18576f7933f6f089196732029" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.766ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>被称为<a href="/wiki/%E7%A9%8D%E5%88%86%E5%B8%B8%E6%95%B8" title="積分常數">积分常数</a>。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E5.BE.AE.E7.A7.AF.E5.88.86.E5.9F.BA.E6.9C.AC.E5.AE.9A.E7.90.86"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="微积分基本定理">微积分基本定理</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%BE%AE%E7%A7%AF%E5%88%86%E5%AD%A6&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="编辑章节：微积分基本定理">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>微积分基本定理（Fundamental Theorem of Calculus）又称微积分基本公式，证实微分和积分互为逆运算。更精确地说，它将一个<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%8F%8D%E5%B0%8E%E6%95%B8" title="反導數">反导数</a>的具体值与定积分联系起来。因为计算反导数通常比应用定积分定义更加简单，微积分基本公式为计算定积分提供了一个行之有效的方式。它也可以被理解为微分是积分逆运算的精确解释。
</p><p>微积分基本公式：如果函數<i>f</i>在<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \left[a,\;b\right]}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mrow>
<mo>[</mo>
<mrow>
<mi>a</mi>
<mo>,</mo>
<mspace width="thickmathspace"></mspace>
<mi>b</mi>
</mrow>
<mo>]</mo>
</mrow>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \left[a,\;b\right]}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle \left[a,\;b\right]}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/3641c60e154afb0ae06179bc3e6af9721d719c2e" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:5.2ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span>区间是<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%BF%9E%E7%BB%AD" title="连续">连续</a>的，函數<i>F</i>在区间(<i>a</i>, <i>b</i>)的导数是<i>f</i>，那么，
設 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle f(x)=F(x)+C.}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</p><p><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \int _{a}^{b}f'(x)\,\mathrm {d} x=f(b)-f(a).}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle \int f'(x)\,\mathrm {d} x=F(x)+C=F(x)+f(a)-F(a)=f(x),{\text{where }}C=f(a)-F(a),a,C\in \mathbf {R} .}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/0ab3281f24338d79e1544b203e803bd617579018" style="vertical-align: -2.338ex; width:88.511ex; height:5.676ex;"/></span>
</p><p><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle {\frac {d}{dx}}\int _{a}^{x}f(t)\,dt=f(x).}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle {\frac {d}{dx}}\int _{a}^{x}f(t)\,dt=f(x).}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle {\frac {d}{dx}}\int _{a}^{x}f(t)\,dt=f(x).}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/bf4f64cc882e88a4d7b634c37b7c1684630c3687" style="vertical-align: -2.338ex; width:22.325ex; height:5.843ex;"/></span>
</p><p>这成为日后数学分析硕果的重要基石。基本公式为计算定积分提供了简单的计算<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%8F%8D%E5%B0%8E%E6%95%B8" title="反導數">反导数</a>的代数方法，而无须使用其极限定義来計算。它也是解<a href="/wiki/%E5%BE%AE%E5%88%86%E6%96%B9%E7%A8%8B" title="微分方程">微分方程</a>的雏形。<a href="/wiki/%E5%BE%AE%E5%88%86%E6%96%B9%E7%A8%8B" title="微分方程">微分方程</a>把一個未知函數與其导数相關連，而在科学的不同領域中，微分方程都很常見。
</p>
<h2><span id=".E5.BE.AE.E7.A9.8D.E5.88.86.E7.9A.84.E7.AC.A6.E8.99.9F"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="微積分的符號">微積分的符號</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%BE%AE%E7%A7%AF%E5%88%86%E5%AD%A6&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="编辑章节：微積分的符號">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>微分學中的符號「<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle {\textrm {d}}x}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mtext>d</mtext>
</mrow>
</mrow>
<mi>x</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle {\textrm {d}}x}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\textrm{d}x" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/b66391c36f741b9bae636f66df2ba744bd46ff40" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:2.622ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>」、「<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle {\textrm {d}}y}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mtext>d</mtext>
</mrow>
</mrow>
<mi>y</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle {\textrm {d}}y}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\textrm{d}y" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/e3c07726a17e7178d70b95a6b599104379b3ed46" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:2.448ex; height:2.509ex;"/></span>」等，是由萊布尼茨首先使用。其中的<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle {\textrm {d}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mtext>d</mtext>
</mrow>
</mrow>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle {\textrm {d}}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\textrm{d}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/59fec77b0a438385764e209260d36a99196028f0" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.293ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>源自<a href="/wiki/%E6%8B%89%E4%B8%81%E8%AF%AD" title="拉丁语">拉丁语</a>中「差」（Differentia）的第一個字母。積分符號「<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \int _{}\,}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<msub>
<mo>∫<!-- ∫ --></mo>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
</mrow>
</msub>
<mspace width="thinmathspace"></mspace>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \int _{}\,}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\int_{}\," aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/e2337d9aa29479e95a5d4ddf06f6244c858c2e13" style="vertical-align: -2.338ex; width:2.581ex; height:5.676ex;"/></span>」亦由萊布尼茨所創，它是拉丁语「總和」（Summa）的第一個字母s的伸長（和<a href="/wiki/%CE%A3" title="Σ">Σ</a>有相同的意義）。
</p>
<h2><span id=".E5.BE.AE.E7.A9.8D.E5.88.86.E5.AD.B8.E7.9A.84.E6.87.89.E7.94.A8"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="微積分學的應用">微積分學的應用</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%BE%AE%E7%A7%AF%E5%88%86%E5%AD%A6&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="编辑章节：微積分學的應用">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:NautilusCutawayLogarithmicSpiral.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1693" data-file-width="2240" decoding="async" height="166" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/08/NautilusCutawayLogarithmicSpiral.jpg/220px-NautilusCutawayLogarithmicSpiral.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/08/NautilusCutawayLogarithmicSpiral.jpg/330px-NautilusCutawayLogarithmicSpiral.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/08/NautilusCutawayLogarithmicSpiral.jpg/440px-NautilusCutawayLogarithmicSpiral.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:NautilusCutawayLogarithmicSpiral.jpg" title="放大"></a></div><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%B9%A6%E9%B9%89%E8%9E%BA" title="鹦鹉螺">鹦鹉螺</a>的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%AF%B9%E6%95%B0%E8%9E%BA%E7%BA%BF" title="对数螺线">对数螺线</a>是刻劃與微积分相關之增长、变化概念的经典图像</div></div></div>
<p>微積分學的發展與應用幾乎影響了現代生活的所有領域。它與大部分<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%A7%91%E5%AD%B8" title="科學">科學</a>分支關係密切，包括<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%B2%BE%E7%AE%97" title="精算">精算</a>、計算機、統計、工業工程、商業管理、醫藥、護理、人口統計，特別是<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%89%A9%E7%90%86%E5%AD%B8" title="物理學">物理學</a>；<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%B6%93%E6%BF%9F%E5%AD%B8" title="經濟學">經濟學</a>亦經常會用到微積分學。幾乎所有現代科學技術，如：<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%A9%9F%E6%A2%B0" title="機械">機械</a>、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%B0%B4%E5%88%A9" title="水利">水利</a>、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%9C%9F%E6%9C%A8" title="土木">土木</a>、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%BB%BA%E7%AF%89" title="建築">建築</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E8%88%AA%E7%A9%BA" title="航空">航空</a>及<a href="/wiki/%E8%88%AA%E6%B5%B7" title="航海">航海</a>等工業工程都以微積分學作為基本數學工具。微積分使得數學可以在（非常數）變化率和總改變之間互相轉化，讓我們可以在已知其中一者时求出另一者。
</p><p>物理學大量應用微積分；<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%8F%A4%E5%85%B8%E5%8A%9B%E5%AD%B8" title="古典力學">古典力學</a>、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%86%B1%E5%82%B3" title="熱傳">熱傳</a>和<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%9B%BB%E7%A3%81%E5%AD%B8" title="電磁學">電磁學</a>都與微積分有密切聯繫。已知<a href="/wiki/%E5%AF%86%E5%BA%A6" title="密度">密度</a>的物體<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%B3%AA%E9%87%8F" title="質量">質量</a>、物體的<a href="/wiki/%E8%BD%89%E5%8B%95%E6%85%A3%E9%87%8F" title="轉動慣量">轉動慣量</a>、物體在<a href="/wiki/%E4%BF%9D%E5%AE%88%E5%90%91%E9%87%8F%E5%9C%BA" title="保守向量场">保守力場</a>的總能量都可用微積分來計算。<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%89%9B%E9%A0%93%E7%AC%AC%E4%BA%8C%E5%AE%9A%E5%BE%8B" title="牛頓第二定律">牛頓第二定律</a>便是微積分在力學中的一個應用例子：它的最初陳述使用了“變化率”一詞，而“變化率”即是指導數。陳述大意為：物體<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%8B%95%E9%87%8F" title="動量">動量</a>的變化率等於作用在物體上的力，而且朝同一方向。今天常用的表達方式是<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \mathbf {F} =m\mathbf {a} }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi mathvariant="bold">F</mi>
</mrow>
<mo>=</mo>
<mi>m</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi mathvariant="bold">a</mi>
</mrow>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \mathbf {F} =m\mathbf {a} }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\mathbf  {F}}=m{\mathbf  {a}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/d0c60fab89e8c3193952047dc565bcf8d233d115" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:8.121ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span> ，它包括了微分，因為<a href="/wiki/%E5%8A%A0%E9%80%9F%E5%BA%A6" title="加速度">加速度</a>是<a href="/wiki/%E9%80%9F%E5%BA%A6" title="速度">速度</a>的導數，或是<a href="/wiki/%E4%BD%8D%E7%BD%AE%E5%90%91%E9%87%8F" title="位置向量">位置矢量</a>的二階導數。已知物體的加速度，我們就可以得出它的路徑。
</p><p>麦克斯韦尔的<a href="/wiki/%E7%94%B5%E7%A3%81%E5%AD%A6" title="电磁学">电磁学</a>理論和<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%88%B1%E5%9B%A0%E6%96%AF%E5%9D%A6" title="爱因斯坦">爱因斯坦</a>的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%B9%BF%E4%B9%89%E7%9B%B8%E5%AF%B9%E8%AE%BA" title="广义相对论">广义相对论</a>都应用了微分。化学使用微积分来计算反应速率，放射性衰退。生物学用微积分来计算种群动态，输入繁殖率和死亡率来模拟种群改变。
</p><p>微積分可以與其它數學分支並用。例如，可與<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%B7%9A%E6%80%A7%E4%BB%A3%E6%95%B8" title="線性代數">線性代數</a>並用，來求得某區域中一組點的“最佳”線性近似。它也可以用在<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%A6%82%E7%8E%87%E8%AB%96" title="概率論">概率論</a>中，來確定由給定密度函數所給出的连续隨機變量之概率。在<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%A7%A3%E6%9E%90%E5%B9%BE%E4%BD%95" title="解析幾何">解析幾何</a>對函數圖像的研究中，微積分可以用來求得最大值、最小值、斜率、<a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%87%B9%E5%BA%A6&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="凹度（页面不存在）">凹度</a>、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%8B%90%E9%BB%9E" title="拐點">拐點</a>等。
</p><p><a href="/wiki/%E6%A0%BC%E6%9E%97%E5%85%AC%E5%BC%8F" title="格林公式">格林公式</a>將一個封閉曲線上的線積分，與一個邊界為<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle C}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>C</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle C}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="C" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/4fc55753007cd3c18576f7933f6f089196732029" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.766ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>且平面區域為<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle D}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>D</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle D}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="D" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/f34a0c600395e5d4345287e21fb26efd386990e6" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.924ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>的雙重積分聯繫起來。這一點被應用於<a href="/wiki/%E6%B1%82%E7%A9%8D%E5%84%80" title="求積儀">求積儀</a>這個工具，它用於量度在平面上的不規則圖形面積。例如，它可以在设计住宅擺設时，计算不规则的花瓣床、游泳池所佔的面积。
</p><p>在医疗领域，微积分可以计算血管最优支角，将血流最大化。通过药物在体内的衰退規律，微积分可以推导出服藥規律。
</p><p>在经济学中，微积分可以通过计算<a href="/wiki/%E8%BE%B9%E9%99%85%E6%88%90%E6%9C%AC" title="边际成本">边际成本</a>和<a href="/wiki/%E8%BE%B9%E9%99%85%E6%94%B6%E7%9B%8A" title="边际收益">边际收益</a>来确定最大<a href="/wiki/%E5%88%A9%E6%BD%A4" title="利潤">利潤</a>。
</p><p>微積分也被用於尋找方程的近似值；實踐中，它是在各種應用裡解微分方程、求根的標準做法。典型的方法有<a href="/wiki/%E7%89%9B%E9%A1%BF%E6%B3%95" title="牛顿法">牛頓法</a>、<a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%AE%9A%E9%BB%9E%E8%BF%AD%E4%BB%A3%E6%B3%95&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="定點迭代法（页面不存在）">定點迭代法</a>、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%B7%9A%E6%80%A7%E8%BF%91%E4%BC%BC" title="線性近似">線性近似</a>等。比如：宇宙飛船利用一種<a href="/wiki/%E6%AC%A7%E6%8B%89%E6%96%B9%E6%B3%95" title="欧拉方法">歐拉方法</a>的變體来求得零重力環境下的近似航線。
</p>
<h2><span id=".E5.AD.A6.E7.A7.91.E6.95.99.E8.82.B2"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="学科教育">学科教育</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%BE%AE%E7%A7%AF%E5%88%86%E5%AD%A6&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="编辑章节：学科教育">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>在美国<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%A4%A7%E5%AD%A6%E5%85%88%E4%BF%AE%E8%AF%BE%E7%A8%8B" title="大学先修课程">大学先修课程</a>中，AP微积分AB、BC分别为对应大学一元微积分半年、全年课程。
</p><p>在<a href="/wiki/%E9%A6%99%E6%B8%AF" title="香港">香港</a>，微積分是<a href="/wiki/%E4%B8%89%E4%B8%89%E5%9B%9B%E9%AB%98%E4%B8%AD%E6%95%99%E8%82%B2%E6%94%B9%E9%9D%A9" title="三三四高中教育改革">新高中</a><a href="/wiki/%E6%95%B8%E5%AD%B8%E7%A7%91%E5%BB%B6%E4%BC%B8%E9%83%A8%E5%88%86" title="數學科延伸部分">數學科延伸部分</a>課程的一部份，這部分是選修的。
</p><p>在<a href="/wiki/%E8%87%BA%E7%81%A3" title="臺灣">台灣</a>，普通型高中數學分成「數學甲」與「數學乙」兩種。過去數學甲是自然組數學，三年級下學期才有基礎微積分課程；數學乙是社會組數學，僅有提到極限的概念而已。但自2019年啟用<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/108%E8%AA%B2%E7%B6%B1" title="108課綱">108課綱</a>後，數學甲與數學乙皆從三年級上學期開始教學基礎微積分課程。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-10"><a href="#cite_note-10">[8]</a></sup>技術型高中數學分成「數學A」、「數學B」、「數學C」與「數學S」四種，各四冊。數學A是家政數學；數學B商業數學；數學C是工業工程數學；數學S是影視數學，其中「數學A」、與「數學S」皆並未列入，僅「數學B」、「數學C」才有，並在醫、農、理、工、商管學院大學部一年級上、下學期分別開設「微積分 (一) 」、「微積分 (二) 」課程，作為該學院之共同必修課程，也為該學院之各科系將來開設之進階課程奠定基礎，以方便學生修習，同時，也是熱門大學轉學考及碩士班考試，熱門考科之一。
</p>
<h2><span id=".E5.8F.83.E8.A6.8B"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="參見">參見</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%BE%AE%E7%A7%AF%E5%88%86%E5%AD%A6&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="编辑章节：參見">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

<h2><span id=".E5.A4.96.E9.83.A8.E9.93.BE.E6.8E.A5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="外部链接">外部链接</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%BE%AE%E7%A7%AF%E5%88%86%E5%AD%A6&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="编辑章节：外部链接">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

<ul><li>数学的领域也可根据“<a href="/wiki/%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6%E5%AD%A6%E7%A7%91%E5%88%86%E7%B1%BB%E6%A0%87%E5%87%86" title="数学学科分类标准">MSC分类标准</a>”或“<a href="/wiki/%E4%B8%AD%E5%9B%BD%E5%AD%A6%E7%A7%91%E5%88%86%E7%B1%BB%E5%9B%BD%E5%AE%B6%E6%A0%87%E5%87%86/110" title="中国学科分类国家标准/110">中国学科分类国家标准</a>”进行分类。</li></ul>

<ul><li><img alt="分类" data-file-height="185" data-file-width="180" decoding="async" height="16" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/96/Symbol_category_class.svg/16px-Symbol_category_class.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/96/Symbol_category_class.svg/23px-Symbol_category_class.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/96/Symbol_category_class.svg/31px-Symbol_category_class.svg.png 2x" title="分类" width="16"/> <b><a href="/wiki/Category:%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6" title="Category:数学">分类</a></b></li>
